# 'di ltar gang du 'dod pa'i sred pa kun du 'byung ba thams cad 'dod pa'i khams su bsdus pa'o / / de dag kyang dbang po'i khams drug dang yul gyi khams drug dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug go /
kati rūpapratisaṃyuktāḥ / caturdaśa / tatra ṣaḍ / cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaindriyadhātavaḥ catvāroviṣayadhātavaḥ tadviṣayavijñānadhātavaś catvāraḥ ete caturdaśa rūpadhātupratisaṃyuktāḥ / kim punaḥ kāraṇaṃgandharasayo rūpadhātau na bhāvas tadvijñānayoś ca / gandharasau hy ekāntenakavaḍīkārāhārasvabhāvāv evana tu sparśavedanāhārasvabhāvau / api cakavaḍīkārāhāravītarāgāś ca rūpadhātāv upapadyanteyadvītarāgāś ca yatropapadyante tatra tasyābhāvaḥ tadyathārūpavītarāgāṇām ārūpyāpattau cakṣurādīnām
# gzugs dang ldan pa du zhe na / / bcu bzhi ste / / mig dang rna ba dang sna dang; lce dang lus dang yid kyi dbang po'i khams dang yul bzhi dang yul de'i rnam par shes pa'i khams bzhi ste / / bcu bzhi po de dag ni gzugs kyi khams dang ldan pa'o / / ci'i phyir gzugs kyi khams na dri dang ro dang de'i rnam par shes pa gnyis kyang med ce na / / dri dang ro ni gcig tu kham gyi zas kyi ngo bo nyid yin gyi reg pa dang sems pa'i zas kyi ngo bo nyid ma yin no / / yang kham gyi zas kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams ni gzugs kyi khams su skye ste / / gang gi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams gang du skyes pa de na med de / / dper na /
viṣayābhāvāc cagandharasavijñānayor apy abhāvaḥ / katy ārūpyapratisaṃyuktāḥ / paścimās / trayaḥ
# 'dod chags dang bral ba gzugs med par skyes pa'i mig la sogs pa bzhin du yul med pa'i phyir dri dang ro'i rnam par shes pa gnyis kyang med do / / gzugs med pa dang ldan pa du zhe na / / tha ma gsum zhes bya ba ni /
manodhātur dharmadhātur manovijñānadhātuś ca
# yid kyi khams dang; chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
rūpavītarāgā hy ārūpyadhātāv utpadyante / atas tatra daśarūpasvabhāvā dhātavas tadāśrayālambanāś ca pañcavijñānadhātavo na santi
# gzugs kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams ni gzugs med pa'i khams su skye ste / / de'i phyir de na gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid kyi khams bcu dang de la brten pa dang dmigs pa rnam par shes pa'i khams lnga med do /
katy apratisaṃyuktāḥ / ye'nāsravāḥ / ye / kāmarūpārūpyatṛṣṇābhir nālambyante / dhātutrayaviyuktatvādapratisaṃyuktāḥ / yemārgasatyāsaṃskṛtasvabhāvāmanodharmamanovijñānadhātavas te 'nāsravāḥ / kati kuśalāḥ / katy akuśalāḥ
# mi ldan pa du zhe na gsum gyi cha'o zhes bya ba ni gang dag 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i sred pa rnams kyis ma dmigs pa ste / / khams gsum dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir mi ldan pa'o / / lam gyi bden pa dang 'dus ma byas kyi ngo bo nyid gang yin pa'i yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams de dag ni zag pa med pa'o / / dge ba du / / mi dge ba du /
katy / avyākṛtāḥ
# lung du ma bstan pa du zhe na /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate
# khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
tatra kutsitāc chalitam iti kuśalam gatam ityarthaḥ
# de la ngan pa bsnyil ba'i phyir dge ba ste / / song zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kuśeti vā prajñāparyāyaḥ / lā ādāne
# yang na ku sha ni shes rab kyi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o / / la ni len pa ste /
prajñāparigṛhītāḥ prajñāparigrāhakā vā kuśalāḥ
# shes rab kyis yongs su zin pa'am / / shes rab yongs su 'dzin pa ni dge ba rnams so /
kutsitena vākāreṇa śerata itikuśāḥ chedakā vedhakāś ceti
# yang na ngan pa'i rnam par 'dug pa ni rtsva ku sha ste / / gcod pa dang 'bigs pa'o /
lā ādāne / yaśchedanavedhanaparihāreṇa kuśān ādatte sa kuśala ity ucyate
# la ni len pa ste / / su zhig gcod pa dang 'bigs pa spangs te / / rtsva ku sha rnams len pa de ni mkhas pa zhes bya'o /
evam anyo 'pi yasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ praśaṃsām arhati sa kuśalastatrocyate
# de bzhin du gzhan bya ba gang la bsngags par 'os pa de ni dge ba zhes bya'o /
etenākuśalaṃ vyākhyātam
# 'dis mi dge ba bzlog ste bshad do /
kuśalākuśalabhāvenāvyākaraṇād avyākṛtāḥ
# dge ba dang mi dge ba'i dngos por lung du bstan pa med pas ma bstan pa'o /
daśa trividhā / iti kuśalā apy akuśalā apy avyākṛtā api / te tu na vijñāyantaaṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ katame daśety āha saptacittadhātavor srūpaśabdadharmadhātavaśceti
# bcu ni rnam pa gsum char te zhes bya ba ni dge ba yang yin / / mi dge ba yang yin / / lung du ma bstan pa yang yin no / / khams pa co brgyad kyi nang nas bcu gang zhes bya ba de dag kyang mi shes nas / / sems kyi khams bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams so zhes bya ba smos so /
atra cittadhātūnāṃ samprayogataḥ kuśalākuśalatvam na svataḥ kuśalākuśalamūlānāṃ ceti
# de la sems kyi khams rnams ni mtshungs par ldan pas dge ba dang mi dge ba nyid yin gyi / / ngo bo nyid kyi ni ma yin te / / dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pas so /
tatra sapta cittadhātavo 'lobhādveṣāmohasamprayuktāḥ kuśalāḥ
# de la sems kyi khams bdun ma chags pa dang zhe sdang med pa dang gti mug med pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams ni dge ba'o /
lobhadveṣamohasamprayuktāakuśalāḥ / anya avyākṛtāḥ / rūpaśabdadhātū kuśalākuśalacittasamutthāpitau kuśalākuśalaukāyavāgvijñaptisaṅgṛhītau
# chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams ni mi dge ba'o / / gzhan dag ni lung du ma bstan pa'o / / gzugs dang sgra'i khams lus dang ngag gi rnam par rig byed du bsdus pa dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems kyis kun nas bslang ba ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'o /
ato 'nyāv avyākṛtau
# de las gzhan pa ni lung du ma bstan pa'o /
dharmadhāturalobhādisvabhāvasamprayuktasamutthaḥ pratisaṅkhyānirodhastathatā ca kuśalaḥ
# chos kyi khams kyang ma chags pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang ba dang so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid ni dge ba'o /
lobhādisvabhāvasamprayuktasamuttho'kuśalaḥ / tato'nyo 'vyākṛtaḥ
# chags pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang ba ni mi dge ba'o / / de las gzhan pa ni lung du ma bstan pa'o; /
aṣṭāv avyākṛtāḥ / gandharasasparśāḥ pañca cakṣurādayaḥ
# brgyad ni lung du ma bstan pa ste / / dre dang ro dang reg bya dang mig la sogs pa lnga'o /
ete hyavyākṛtāevapara mārt hasv abhā vasa mpra yo gasamutth ānat a ḥkuśalākuśalatvābhāvāt
# de dag ni lung du ma bstan pa nyid de / / don dam pa dang ngo bo nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang kun nas bslang bas dge ba dang mi dge ba ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
katy ādhyātmikāḥ / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti
# nang gi du zhe na; khams bco brgyad ces bya bar sbyar ro /
sambadhyate / dvādaśa / te tu na prajñāyante katamedvādaśety āha rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyadharmadhāt
# bcu gnyis te bcu gnyis gang yin pa de dag kyang mi shes pas / / gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos kyi khams ma gtogs so zhes bya ba smos so /
ūn sthāpayitveti / śeṣāḥṣaḍ indriyadhātavaḥ ṣaḍvijñānadhātava ity ete dvādaśādhyātmikāḥ
# lhag ma dbang po'i khams drug dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug ste / / bcu gnyis po de dag ni nang gi'o /
kati dhātavo bāhyāḥ / ṣaṭ / te tu na vijñāyanta ity ata āha / ye sthāpitāḥ / ete bāhyā iti boddhavyāḥ / ke ca sthāpitāḥ / rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyadharmadhātavaḥ
# khams rnams las phyi rol gyi du zhe na drug ste / / de dag kyang mi shes nas / / de'i phyir gang dag ma gtogs pa rnams so zhes bya ba smos so / / 'di dag ni phyi'i yin par shes par bya'o / / ma gtogs pa rnams gang zhe na / / gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos kyi khams rnams so /
adhy ātmānam adhyātmam / adhyātmam evādhyātmikam
# bdag gi dbang du byas pa ni nang zhes bya ba ste / / nang nyid nang ngo /
ātmanyasati katham ādhyātmikaṃ bāhyaṃ vābhavati
# bdag nyid med na nang ngam phyi zhes bya bar ji ltar 'gyur te /
na hi śīle 'satyadhiśīlaṃ śikṣā yujyate / ahaṅkārasanniśritatvāc cittam ātmety upacaryate / ahaṅkārasanniśrayo hy ātmavādibhir ātmetyabhidhīyate
# tshul khrims med na tshul khrims kyi dbang du byas pa'i bslab pa mi rung ba bzhin no zhe na / / ngar 'dzin pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir sems la bdag ces 'dogs so / / ngar 'dzin pa'i gzhi ni bdag tu smra ba rnams kyis bdag ces brjod de /
tathā hy ātmaguṇatvenātmaviṣayatvenacāhaṅkāraṃ pratipannāḥ
# 'di ltar bdag gi yon tan nam / / bdag yul nyid du ngar 'dzin pa rtogs so /
ahaṅkāraś ca cittasanniśritastadvyatiriktātmābhāvāt
# ngar 'dzin pa yang sems la brten pa ste / / de las gud na bdag med pa'i phyir ro /
āhito 'haṃmāna etasminn ity ātmā / cittam eva caittānām āśraya iti cittam evātmatvenopacaryate
# de la nga'o snyam du nga rgyal skyed pas bdag ste / / sems nyid sems las byung ba rnams kyi gnas yin pas sems nyid la bdag tu 'dogs so /
kathaṃ punar etad gamyate 'trātmatvena cittam abhipretam iti
# 'dir sems la bdag ces bya bar bzhed par 'di ci mngon zhe na / / bcom ldan 'das kyis /
uktaṃ hi bhagavatā ātmanā hi sudāntena svargaṃ prāpnotipaṇḍitaiti
# bdag ni legs par dul gyur na / / mkhas pas mtho ris thob par 'gyur / / zhes gsungs so /
cittasya cānyatra damanam uktam cittasyadamanaṃ sādhu cittaṃ dāntaṃ sukhāvahamiti
# gzhan nas kyang sems 'dul ba gsungs te / / sems 'dul ba ni legs pa ste / / sems 'dul bde ba thob par byed / / ce'o /
atra hi cittasyadamanaṃ cittam eva dāntaṃ sukhāvaham ity uktam
# 'dir sems 'dul ba dang sems nyid dul na bde ba thob par byed / / ces gsungs pas de'i phyir / / bdag ni legs par dul gyur na /
ato 'trāpy ātmanā hi sudāntena svargaṃ prāpnoti paṇḍita iti cittamevābhipretam iti vijñāyate / ataś cātmabhūtasyacittasyāśrayabhāvena pratyāsannatvāc cakṣurādīnāmādhyātmikatvam
# mkhas pas mtho ris thob par 'gyur / / zhes bya ba 'dir yang sems nyid la bya bar bzhed par mngon no / / de'i phyir bdag tu lta ba'i sems kyi rten gyi dngos por nye bar gyur pa'i phyir mig la sogs pa ni nang gi nyid do /
rūpādīnāṃ ca viṣayabhāvād bāhyatvam
# gzugs la sogs pa yul gyi dngos por gyur pa ni phyi'i nyid do /
evaṃ tarhi ṣaḍ vijñānadhātava ādhyātmikā na prāpnuvanti nahy ete manodhātutvam aprāptāś cittasyāśrayībhavantīti
# de ltar na ni rnam par shes pa'i khams drug nang gir mi 'gyur te / / de dag yid kyi khams nyid du ma gyur gyi bar du sems kyi rten du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhe na /
yadātadā ta eva te bhavantīti lakṣaṇaṃ nātivartantaiti
# nam du yang rung ste / / de dag nyid nad yin pas mtshan nyid las 'da' ba med do /
kati sālambanādhātava iti prakṛtam / ata āha sapteti / te 'pi na jñāyante katamesaptety ata āha cittadhātavaiti
# dmigs pa dang bcas pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams kyi skabs yin pas de'i phyir bdun zhes bya ba smos so / / bdun po de dag kyang gang yin mi shes pas de'i phyir sems kyi khams zhes bya ba smos so /
kim eta eva sālambanāḥ / na kiṃ tarhidharmadhātupradeśaśca
# dmigs pa dang bcas pa 'di dag nyid du zad dam zhe na / / ma yin te / / chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig kyang yin te /
caśabdaḥ samuccaye sapta cittadhātavo dharmadhātupradeśaś ca sālambana iti
# kyang gi sgra ni bsdu'o / / sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams kyi gcig kyang dmigs pa dang bcas pa yin te /
astyamīṣām ālambanam iti sālambanāḥ
# 'di dag la dmigs pa yod pas dmigs pa dang bcas pa'o /
viṣayo gocara ālambanamiti paryāyāḥ / sapta cittadhātavaścakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyamanovijñānamanodhātavodharmadhātupradeśaś ca yaścaitasikasvabhāvaḥ
# yul dang spyod yul dang dmigs pa zhes bya ba rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o / / sems kyi khams bdun ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa rnams so / / chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig ni gang sems las byung ba'i ngo bo nyid do /
katy anālambanāḥ
# dmigs pa med pa du zhe na /
śeṣāḥ / te punar daśa / pañcendriyadhātavaś cakṣurādayaḥ pañca viṣayadhātavorūpādayo dharmadhātupradeśaś cayo nacaitasikasvabhāvaḥ
# lhag ma rnams te / / de dag kyang bcu ste / / mig la sogs pa dbang po'i khams lnga dang gzugs la sogs pa yul gyi khams lnga'o / / chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gang sems las byung ba'i ngo bo nyid ma yin pa'o /
kati vikalpakāḥ / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti
# rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa du zhe na / / khams bco brgyad ces bya bar sbyar ro /
sambadhyate / manodhātur manovijñānadhāturdharmadhātoś ca pradeśoyaḥ samprayuktaḥ
# yid kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang; chos kyi khams kyi phyogs so zhes bya ba ni gang mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
etau / hy abhinirūpaṇānusmaraṇavikalpābhyāṃ samprayuktau tāveva vikalpakau netarau tābhyām asamprayogāt
# 'di gnyis ni mngon par dpyod pa dang rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ste / / de nyid rnam par rtog pa yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin te /
dharmadhātupradeśo 'pi samprayuktaḥ netaraḥ / tatrānusmaraṇavikalpaḥ smṛtir eva mānasy anub hūtā lamb anās ampr amoṣ ākār ā
# de gnyis dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / chos kyi khams kyi phyogs ni mtshungs par ldan pa can te / / gzhan ni ma yin no / / de la rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni dran pa nyid la bya ste / / yid kyi myong ba'i dmigs pa ma brjed pa rnams so /
traiyadhvikaparokṣārthābhyūhanākāra idam evaṃ naivam itiprajñāviśeṣaś cetanā vā 'bhirūpaṇāvikalpaḥ
# dus gsum gyi don lkog tu gyur pa la mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam pa 'di ni 'di lta yin gyi de lta ma yin no zhes bya ba shes rab kyi khyad par la'am / / sems pa ni mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa ste /
yathoktam abhidharmasamuccaye anusmaraṇavikalpaḥ katamaḥ / yo'nubhūtapūrvasaṃskārākāraḥ
# chos mngon pa kun las btus pa las ji skad du / / rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang zhe na / / gang sngon myong ba la 'du byed bskyed pa'o /
abhinirūpaṇāvikalpaḥ katamaḥ
# mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang zhe na /
yo 'tītānāgatavartamāneṣu viparokṣeṣv abhyūhanākārovikalpaḥ / śeṣā avikalpakā iti siddham
# gang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi don lkog tu gyur pa rnams la mngon par dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o zhes bshad pa lta bu'o / / lhag ma rnams ni rnam par mi rtog par 'grub ste /
te punaḥ pañcadaśa dhātavo
# de dag kyang khams bco lnga ste /
dharmadhātoś ca pradeśaḥ
# chos kyi khams kyi phyogs te /
ete hy avikalpakā eva
# de dag ni rnam par mi rtog pa nyid do /
aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃkaty upāttāḥ / pañcādhyātmikāḥ / te punaścakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyadhātavaḥ
# khams bco brgyad las zin pa du zhe na / / nang gi lnga ste / / de dag ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams te /
ete hy upāttā eva
# de dag ni zin pa nyid do /
nanu cānyatraite dvidhā nirdiṣṭāḥ
# gzhan las 'di dag gnyis su ma bstan tam /
satyaṃ nirdiṣṭāḥ tatra hyatītānāgatā anupāttāuktāḥ te ca na santy eva
# bstan mod kyi de la yang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa ni zin pa ma yin par brjod de / / de ni med pa nyid do /
na cāsataupāttatvam anupāttatvaṃ vā yujyate
# med pa ni zin pa'am ma zin pa yin par brjod du mi rung ngo /
vartamānās tusvasattādhyāsitatvāt cittacaittaiś copāttatvād upāttā evacakṣurādayaḥ nānupāttāḥ / kiṃ cakṣurādaya eva pañcopāttāḥ
# da ltar ni rang yod par gnas pa dang sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyis zin pa'i phyir zin pa nyid de / / mig la sogs pa ni ma zin pa ma yin no / / ci mig la sogs pa lnga po nyid zin pa dag gang zhe na /
na kiṃ tarhi caturṇāṃ ca pradeśaḥ
# ma yin te / / bzhi'i phyogs te /
katameṣāṃcaturṇām ity atra āha rūparasagandhaspraṣṭavyānām iti / tatra ye
# bzhi po de dag gang yin snyam pa la de'i phyir / / gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya rnams kyi'o zhes bya ba smos so /
srūpagandharasaspraṣṭavyadhātava indriyāvinirbhāgavartinaḥte indriyavad upāttāḥ
# de la gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya'i khams dbang po las tha dad du mi 'jug pa gang dag yin pa de dag dbang po dag bzhin du zin pa rnams so / / gzhan dag ni ma zin pa dag ste /
anye 'nupāttāḥ tadyathā mūlavarjyeṣukeśaromanakhadanteṣu viṇmūtrakheṭasiṅghāṇakaśoṇitādiṣubhūmyudakādiṣu ca
# 'di lta ste / / drung ma gtogs pa'i skra dang spu dang sen mo dang so dang phyi sa dang gcin dang mchil ma dang snabs dang khrag la sogs pa dang sa dang chu la sogs pa rnams so /
upāttam iti ko 'rthaḥ
# zin pa zhes bya ba'i don ci zhe na /
yac cittacaittairadhiṣṭhānabhāvenopagṛhītam anugrahopaghātābhyāmanyonyānuvidhānāt / yal lokesacetanam ity ucyate
# phan pa dang gnod pa gnyis kyis phan tshun rjes su 'gyur ba'i phyir gang sems dang sems las byung ba de rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas kyi dngos por zin pa dang 'jig rten na sems bcas pa zhes bya'o /
katy anupāttāḥ
# zin pa ma yin pa du zhe na /
śeṣā navacaturṇāṃ ca / pradeśaḥ / upayuktebhyo ye 'nye te śeṣāḥ / ataḥsaptacittadhātavo dharmadhātuḥ śabdadhātuś ca / caturṇāṃ capradeśa iti rūpagandharasasparśānām
# lhag ma dgu dang bzhi'i phyogs zhes bya ba ni bshad zin pa rnams las gzhan gang yin pa de dag lhag ma'o / / de'i phyir sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams dang sgra'i khams so; / / bzhi'i phyogs zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg pa rnams kyi'o /
sa punar yaindriyāvinirbhāgavartinaṃ bhāgaṃ sthāpayitvā mūlavarjyeṣu keśaromādiṣu vartate
# de yang dbang po dang tha dad du mi 'jug pa'i cha ma gtogs pa dang drung ma gtogs pa'i skra dang spu la sogs pa yod pa'o /
kati sabhāgāḥ / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti prakṛtatvād / abhisambadhyate
# sten pa mtshungs pa du zhe na / / khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
tepañcādhyātmikā iti / dvādaśādhyātmikā uktāḥ / teṣāṃ na vijñāyate katamepañcetyata āha rūpiṇaiti te punaś cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanasparśanadhātavaḥ
# nang gi gzugs can lnga zhes bya ba ni nang gi bcu gnyis bstan pas de dag gi nang na gang yin pa gtol med pas lnga zhes bya ba smos so / / gzugs can zhes bya ba de dag ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi khams so /
kasya sabhāgāḥ kena prakāreṇa sabhāgā iti na vijñāyate ata āha svavijñānair viṣayasāmānyatām upādāyeti / tatra cakṣuṣaḥ svavijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānam / tena svavijñānena cakṣuḥ svaviṣayeṇa rūpeṇa samānam
# gang gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang rnam pa gang gis sten pa mtshungs pa yang mi shes pas de'i phyir / / rang gi rnam par shes pa dag dang yul thun mong ba nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba smos so / / de la mig gi rang gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / rang gi rnam par shes pa de dang mig rang gi yul gzugs su mtshungs te /
dvayor api cakṣurvijñānotpattāv anuguṇatvāt samānam
# gnyi ga yang / / mig gi rnam par shes pa skye ba dang mthun pa'i phyir mtshungs pa'o /
sāmānyatāmupādāyeti gṛhītvā cakṣuḥ svaviṣayeṇa rūpeṇa sabhāgam ucyate
# thun mong pa nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba ni bzung ba ste / / mig gi rang gi yul gzugs dang sten pa mtshungs pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ śrotrādīnām api svaviṣayaiḥ sabhāgatā vaktavyā / etaduktaṃ bhavati ye cakṣurādayaḥ svavijñānair adhyāsitāḥ tesabhāgāḥ
# de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa yang / / rang gi yul rnams dang sten pa mtshungs pa zhes brjod par bya'o / / de ni 'di skad du / / mig la sogs pa gang dag rang gi rnam par shes pa rnams dang gnas pa de dag sten pa mtshungs pa zhes bstan par 'gyur ro; / / de dag dang mtshungs pa du zhe na /
taeva cakṣurādayaḥ svavijñānaśūnyās / tatsabhāgāḥ
# mig la sogs pa de dag nyid rang gi rnam par shes pas stong pa nyid de de dag dang mtshungs pa'o /
kimarthaṃ punas te tatsabhāgā ity ucyante
# ci'i phyir de dag ni de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes bya zhe na /
svajātisāmānyatām upādāyeti
# rang gi rigs dang mthun pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ste /
svavijñānaśūnyāś / cakṣurādayas te sabhāgānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ cakṣurādijātyāsamānā iti taiḥ sadṛśatvāt tatsabhāgā ity ucyante
# rang gi rnam par shes pa stong pa'i mig la sogs pa de dag ni sten pa mtshungs pa'i mig la sogs pa dang mig la sogs par ris mthun pa ste / / de dag dang 'dra ba'i phyir de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes bya'o /
ete hyasādhāraṇatvād ya ekasya sabhāgās tatsabhāgā vā tesarvasattvānām apīti niyatam eṣāṃ sabhāgatatsabhāgatvam
# de dag ni thun mong ma yin pa'i phyir gcig gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs pa gang yin pa de dag ni / / sems can thams cad kyi yang yin pas / / 'di dag gi sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa ni nges pa'o /
rūpādīnāṃ tu pratisantāne sabhāgatatsabhāgatvam itynavasthitam
# gzugs la sogs pa ni so so'i rgyud la sten pa mtshungs pa dang de dag dang mtshungs pa nyid du gnas so /
na ca vijñānād anyat kāritram astīti nānyeṣāṃsabhāgatatsabhāgatvam uktam
# rnam par shes pa las byed pa gzhan med pa'i phyir / / gzhan dag la ni sten pa mtshungs pa de dang de dag dang mtshungs pa zhes ma brjod do /
pañcaskandhakavibhāṣā samāptā
# phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa /
kṛtir ācāryasthiramateḥ
# slob dpon blo gros brtan pa sthi ra ma tis mdzad pa rdzogs so /
